    <script>
     function r(f){/in/.test(document.readyState)?setTimeout('r('+f+')',9):f()}
 var BBIPOPOVER=new function(){var BBI=this;var $=jQuery;var t=false;var timestamp=false;this.init=function(){var params=this.getSearchParameters();if(params.popdemo==1){BBI.show();}
 BBI.timestamp=new Date().getTime();setInterval(function(){BBI.check();},5000);if(window.console){console.groupCollapsed('BBI POPOVER PLUGIN');console.info('Initialised');}}
 this.check=function(){if(BBI.t==true)return;if(window.console){console.info('checking...');}
 $.ajax({type:"GET",url:"index.php",data:'option=com_ajax&module=bbirealestateajax&method=checkUpdate&format=raw&timestamp='+BBI.timestamp,success:function(res){var res=JSON.parse(res);if(res.data==true){BBI.show();BBI.t=true;}else{BBI.timestamp=res.timestamp;}}});}
 this.show=function(){var modal=$('#plg_bbi_popover');if(modal.length<=0){if(!window.console)return;console.error('Modal Element is missing!');return;}
 modal.modal();}
 this.getSearchParameters=function(){var prmstr=window.location.search.substr(1);return prmstr!=null&&prmstr!=""?this.transformToAssocArray(prmstr):{};}
 this.transformToAssocArray=function(prmstr){var params={};var prmarr=prmstr.split("&");for(var i=0;i<prmarr.length;i++){var tmparr=prmarr[i].split("=");params[tmparr[0]]=tmparr[1];}
 return params;}}
 r(function(){if(typeof(window.jQuery)=="undefined"){if(!window.console)return;console.error('jQuery is missing!');return;}else
 if(typeof(jQuery.fn.modal)=="undefined"){if(!window.console)return;console.error('Bootstrap Modal Plugin is missing!');return;}else{BBIPOPOVER.init();}});
    </script>
